**Title:** RotatingMachine

|                           |                                                                           |
| ------------------------- | ------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| **Type**                  | `object`                                                                  |
| **Required**              | No                                                                        |
| **Additional properties** | [[Any type: allowed]](# "Additional Properties of any type are allowed.") |

**Description:** A rotating machine which may be used as a generator or motor.

| Property                                                                                      | Pattern | Type             | Deprecated | Definition                                                                                                                                           | Title/Description                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     |

| - [RotatingMachine.GeneratingUnit](#RotatingMachineGeneratingUnit )                           | No      | object           | No         | In ./GeneratingUnit.json                                                                                                                             | A single or set of synchronous machines for converting mechanical power into alternating-current power. For example, individual machines within a set may be defined for scheduling purposes while a single control signal is derived for the set. In this case there would be a GeneratingUnit for each member of the set and an additional GeneratingUnit corresponding to the set. |

#### <a name="ConductingEquipmentTerminals_items_ACDCTerminalconnected"></a>4.1.1. Property `RotatingMachine > ConductingEquipment.Terminals > Terminal > ACDCTerminal.connected`

**Title:** connected

|              |           |
| ------------ | --------- |
| **Type**     | `boolean` |
| **Required** | No        |

**Description:** The connected status is related to a bus-branch model and the topological node to terminal relation.  True implies the terminal is connected to the related topological node and false implies it is not. 
In a bus-branch model, the connected status is used to tell if equipment is disconnected without having to change the connectivity described by the topological node to terminal relation. A valid case is that conducting equipment can be connected in one end and open in the other. In particular for an AC line segment, where the reactive line charging can be significant, this is a relevant case.

#### <a name="ConductingEquipmentTerminals_items_Terminalphases"></a>4.1.2. Property `RotatingMachine > ConductingEquipment.Terminals > Terminal > Terminal.phases`

**Title:** phases

|                |                    |
| -------------- | ------------------ |
| **Type**       | `enum (of string)` |
| **Required**   | No                 |
| **Defined in** | ./PhaseCode.json   |

**Description:** Represents the normal network phasing condition. If the attribute is missing, three phases (ABC) shall be assumed, except for terminals of grounding classes (specializations of EarthFaultCompensator, GroundDisconnector, and Ground) which will be assumed to be N. Therefore, phase code ABCN is explicitly declared when needed, e.g. for star point grounding equipment.
The phase code on terminals connecting same ConnectivityNode or same TopologicalNode as well as for equipment between two terminals shall be consistent.

Must be one of:
* "ABCN"
* "ABC"
* "ABN"
* "ACN"
* "BCN"
* "AB"
* "AC"
* "BC"
* "AN"
* "BN"
* "CN"
* "A"
* "B"
* "C"
* "N"
* "s1N"
* "s2N"
* "s12N"
* "s1"
* "s2"
* "s12"
* "none"
* "X"
* "XY"
* "XN"
* "XYN"

#### <a name="ConductingEquipmentTerminals_items_ACDCTerminalsequenceNumber"></a>4.1.3. Property `RotatingMachine > ConductingEquipment.Terminals > Terminal > ACDCTerminal.sequenceNumber`

**Title:** sequenceNumber

|              |           |
| ------------ | --------- |
| **Type**     | `integer` |
| **Required** | No        |

**Description:** The orientation of the terminal connections for a multiple terminal conducting equipment.  The sequence numbering starts with 1 and additional terminals should follow in increasing order.   The first terminal is the "starting point" for a two terminal branch.

#### <a name="ConductingEquipmentTerminals_items_IdentifiedObjectdescription"></a>4.1.4. Property `RotatingMachine > ConductingEquipment.Terminals > Terminal > IdentifiedObject.description`

**Title:** description

|              |          |
| ------------ | -------- |
| **Type**     | `string` |
| **Required** | No       |

**Description:** The description is a free human readable text describing or naming the object. It may be non unique and may not correlate to a naming hierarchy.

#### <a name="ConductingEquipmentTerminals_items_IdentifiedObjectaliasName"></a>4.1.5. Property `RotatingMachine > ConductingEquipment.Terminals > Terminal > IdentifiedObject.aliasName`

**Title:** aliasName

|              |          |
| ------------ | -------- |
| **Type**     | `string` |
| **Required** | No       |

**Description:** The aliasName is free text human readable name of the object alternative to IdentifiedObject.name. It may be non unique and may not correlate to a naming hierarchy.
The attribute aliasName is retained because of backwards compatibility between CIM relases. It is however recommended to replace aliasName with the Name class as aliasName is planned for retirement at a future time.

#### <a name="ConductingEquipmentTerminals_items_IdentifiedObjectmRID"></a>4.1.6. Property `RotatingMachine > ConductingEquipment.Terminals > Terminal > IdentifiedObject.mRID`

**Title:** mRID

|              |          |
| ------------ | -------- |
| **Type**     | `string` |
| **Required** | No       |

**Description:** Master resource identifier issued by a model authority. The mRID is unique within an exchange context. Global uniqueness is easily achieved by using a UUID, as specified in RFC 4122, for the mRID. The use of UUID is strongly recommended.
For CIMXML data files in RDF syntax conforming to IEC 61970-552, the mRID is mapped to rdf:ID or rdf:about attributes that identify CIM object elements.

#### <a name="ConductingEquipmentTerminals_items_IdentifiedObjectname"></a>4.1.7. Property `RotatingMachine > ConductingEquipment.Terminals > Terminal > IdentifiedObject.name`

**Title:** name

|              |          |
| ------------ | -------- |
| **Type**     | `string` |
| **Required** | No       |

**Description:** The name is any free human readable and possibly non unique text naming the object.

## <a name="RotatingMachineGeneratingUnit"></a>5. Property `RotatingMachine > RotatingMachine.GeneratingUnit`

|                           |                                                                           |
| ------------------------- | ------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| **Type**                  | `combining`                                                               |
| **Required**              | No                                                                        |
| **Additional properties** | [[Any type: allowed]](# "Additional Properties of any type are allowed.") |
| **Defined in**            | ./GeneratingUnit.json                                                     |

**Description:** A single or set of synchronous machines for converting mechanical power into alternating-current power. For example, individual machines within a set may be defined for scheduling purposes while a single control signal is derived for the set. In this case there would be a GeneratingUnit for each member of the set and an additional GeneratingUnit corresponding to the set.

| One of(Option)                                                        |
| --------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| [HydroGeneratingUnit.json](#RotatingMachineGeneratingUnit_oneOf_i0)   |
| [SolarGeneratingUnit.json](#RotatingMachineGeneratingUnit_oneOf_i1)   |
| [NuclearGeneratingUnit.json](#RotatingMachineGeneratingUnit_oneOf_i2) |
| [WindGeneratingUnit.json](#RotatingMachineGeneratingUnit_oneOf_i3)    |
| [ThermalGeneratingUnit.json](#RotatingMachineGeneratingUnit_oneOf_i4) |

### <a name="RotatingMachineGeneratingUnit_oneOf_i0"></a>5.1. Property `RotatingMachine > RotatingMachine.GeneratingUnit > oneOf > HydroGeneratingUnit.json`

|                           |                                                                           |
| ------------------------- | ------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| **Type**                  | `object`                                                                  |
| **Required**              | No                                                                        |
| **Additional properties** | [[Any type: allowed]](# "Additional Properties of any type are allowed.") |
| **Defined in**            | ./HydroGeneratingUnit.json                                                |

**Description:** A generating unit whose prime mover is a hydraulic turbine (e.g., Francis, Pelton, Kaplan).

#### <a name="RotatingMachineGeneratingUnit_oneOf_i0_GeneratingUnitGenUnitOpSchedule"></a>5.1.1. Property `RotatingMachine > RotatingMachine.GeneratingUnit > oneOf > HydroGeneratingUnit > GeneratingUnit.GenUnitOpSchedule`

|                           |                                                                           |
| ------------------------- | ------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| **Type**                  | `object`                                                                  |
| **Required**              | No                                                                        |
| **Additional properties** | [[Any type: allowed]](# "Additional Properties of any type are allowed.") |
| **Defined in**            | ./GenUnitOpSchedule.json                                                  |

**Description:** The generating unit's Operator-approved current operating schedule (or plan), typically produced with the aid of unit commitment type analyses. The X-axis represents absolute time. The Y1-axis represents the status (0=off-line and unavailable: 1=available: 2=must run: 3=must run at fixed power value: etc.). The Y2-axis represents the must run fixed power value where required.

| Property                                                                                                                                                   | Pattern | Type             | Deprecated | Definition                                                                                                                                                       | Title/Description |
| ---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- | ------- | ---------------- | ---------- | ---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- | ----------------- |
| - [IdentifiedObject.aliasName](#RotatingMachineGeneratingUnit_oneOf_i0_GeneratingUnitGenUnitOpSchedule_IdentifiedObjectaliasName )                         | No      | string           | No         | -                                                                                                                                                                | aliasName         |
| - [BasicIntervalSchedule.value2Multiplier](#RotatingMachineGeneratingUnit_oneOf_i0_GeneratingUnitGenUnitOpSchedule_BasicIntervalSchedulevalue2Multiplier ) | No      | enum (of string) | No         | In ./UnitMultiplier.json                                                                                                                                         | value2Multiplier  |
| - [RegularIntervalSchedule.timeStep](#RotatingMachineGeneratingUnit_oneOf_i0_GeneratingUnitGenUnitOpSchedule_RegularIntervalScheduletimeStep )             | No      | object or number | No         | In ./Seconds.json                                                                                                                                                | timeStep          |
| - [BasicIntervalSchedule.startTime](#RotatingMachineGeneratingUnit_oneOf_i0_GeneratingUnitGenUnitOpSchedule_BasicIntervalSchedulestartTime )               | No      | string           | No         | -                                                                                                                                                                | startTime         |
| - [BasicIntervalSchedule.value1Multiplier](#RotatingMachineGeneratingUnit_oneOf_i0_GeneratingUnitGenUnitOpSchedule_BasicIntervalSchedulevalue1Multiplier ) | No      | enum (of string) | No         | Same as [BasicIntervalSchedule.value2Multiplier](#RotatingMachineGeneratingUnit_oneOf_i0_GeneratingUnitGenUnitOpSchedule_BasicIntervalSchedulevalue2Multiplier ) | value1Multiplier  |
| - [BasicIntervalSchedule.value1Unit](#RotatingMachineGeneratingUnit_oneOf_i0_GeneratingUnitGenUnitOpSchedule_BasicIntervalSchedulevalue1Unit )             | No      | enum (of string) | No         | Same as [unit](#RotatingMachineGeneratingUnit_oneOf_i0_GeneratingUnitGenUnitOpSchedule_RegularIntervalScheduletimeStep_unit )                                    | value1Unit        |
| - [BasicIntervalSchedule.value2Unit](#RotatingMachineGeneratingUnit_oneOf_i0_GeneratingUnitGenUnitOpSchedule_BasicIntervalSchedulevalue2Unit )             | No      | enum (of string) | No         | Same as [unit](#RotatingMachineGeneratingUnit_oneOf_i0_GeneratingUnitGenUnitOpSchedule_RegularIntervalScheduletimeStep_unit )                                    | value2Unit        |
| - [IdentifiedObject.description](#RotatingMachineGeneratingUnit_oneOf_i0_GeneratingUnitGenUnitOpSchedule_IdentifiedObjectdescription )                     | No      | string           | No         | -                                                                                                                                                                | description       |

##### <a name="RotatingMachineGeneratingUnit_oneOf_i0_GeneratingUnitGenUnitOpSchedule_IdentifiedObjectaliasName"></a>5.1.1.1. Property `RotatingMachine > RotatingMachine.GeneratingUnit > oneOf > HydroGeneratingUnit > GeneratingUnit.GenUnitOpSchedule > IdentifiedObject.aliasName`

**Title:** aliasName

|              |          |
| ------------ | -------- |
| **Type**     | `string` |
| **Required** | No       |

**Description:** The aliasName is free text human readable name of the object alternative to IdentifiedObject.name. It may be non unique and may not correlate to a naming hierarchy.
The attribute aliasName is retained because of backwards compatibility between CIM relases. It is however recommended to replace aliasName with the Name class as aliasName is planned for retirement at a future time.

#### <a name="RotatingMachineGeneratingUnit_oneOf_i0_GeneratingUnitGenUnitOpCostCurves"></a>5.1.2. Property `RotatingMachine > RotatingMachine.GeneratingUnit > oneOf > HydroGeneratingUnit > GeneratingUnit.GenUnitOpCostCurves`

The operating cost curve for thermal units is derived from heat input and fuel costs. The operating cost curve for hydro units is derived from water flow rates and equivalent water costs. |

#### <a name="RotatingMachineGeneratingUnit_oneOf_i0_GeneratingUnitgovernorSCD"></a>5.1.4. Property `RotatingMachine > RotatingMachine.GeneratingUnit > oneOf > HydroGeneratingUnit > GeneratingUnit.governorSCD`

**Title:** governorSCD

|                |                    |
| -------------- | ------------------ |
| **Type**       | `object or number` |
| **Required**   | No                 |
| **Defined in** | ./PerCent.json     |

**Description:** Governor Speed Changer Droop.   This is the change in generator power output divided by the change in frequency normalized by the nominal power of the generator and the nominal frequency and expressed in percent and negated. A positive value of speed change droop provides additional generator output upon a drop in frequency.

| - [unit](#RotatingMachineGeneratingUnit_oneOf_i0_GeneratingUnitgovernorSCD_unit )             | No      | enum (of string) | No         | Same as [unit](#RotatingMachineGeneratingUnit_oneOf_i0_GeneratingUnitGenUnitOpSchedule_RegularIntervalScheduletimeStep_unit )                                    | nan                                  |
| - [value](#RotatingMachineGeneratingUnit_oneOf_i0_GeneratingUnitgovernorSCD_value )           | No      | number           | No         | -                                                                                                                                                                | Normally 0 to 100 on a defined base. |

#### <a name="RotatingMachineGeneratingUnit_oneOf_i0_GeneratingUnitnominalP"></a>5.1.19. Property `RotatingMachine > RotatingMachine.GeneratingUnit > oneOf > HydroGeneratingUnit > GeneratingUnit.nominalP`

**Title:** nominalP

|                        |                                                                                                           |
| ---------------------- | --------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| **Type**               | `object or number`                                                                                        |
| **Required**           | No                                                                                                        |
| **Same definition as** | [GeneratingUnit.highControlLimit](#RotatingMachineGeneratingUnit_oneOf_i0_GeneratingUnithighControlLimit) |

**Description:** The nominal power of the generating unit.  Used to give precise meaning to percentage based attributes such as the governor speed change droop (governorSCD attribute).

#### <a name="RotatingMachineGeneratingUnit_oneOf_i0_GeneratingUnitnormalPF"></a>5.1.20. Property `RotatingMachine > RotatingMachine.GeneratingUnit > oneOf > HydroGeneratingUnit > GeneratingUnit.normalPF`

**Title:** normalPF

|              |          |
| ------------ | -------- |
| **Type**     | `number` |
| **Required** | No       |

**Description:** Generating unit economic participation factor.  The sum of the participation factors across generating units does not have to sum to one.  It is used for representing distributed slack participation factor. The attribute shall be a positive value or zero.

#### <a name="RotatingMachineGeneratingUnit_oneOf_i0_GeneratingUnitpenaltyFactor"></a>5.1.21. Property `RotatingMachine > RotatingMachine.GeneratingUnit > oneOf > HydroGeneratingUnit > GeneratingUnit.penaltyFactor`

**Title:** penaltyFactor

|              |          |
| ------------ | -------- |
| **Type**     | `number` |
| **Required** | No       |

**Description:** Defined as: 1 / ( 1 - Incremental Transmission Loss); with the Incremental Transmission Loss expressed as a plus or minus value. The typical range of penalty factors is (0.9 to 1.1).

#### <a name="RotatingMachineGeneratingUnit_oneOf_i0_Equipmentaggregate"></a>5.1.34. Property `RotatingMachine > RotatingMachine.GeneratingUnit > oneOf > HydroGeneratingUnit > Equipment.aggregate`

**Title:** aggregate

|              |           |
| ------------ | --------- |
| **Type**     | `boolean` |
| **Required** | No        |

**Description:** The aggregate flag provides an alternative way of representing an aggregated (equivalent) element. It is applicable in cases when the dedicated classes for equivalent equipment do not have all of the attributes necessary to represent the required level of detail.  In case the flag is set to “true” the single instance of equipment represents multiple pieces of equipment that have been modelled together as an aggregate equivalent obtained by a network reduction procedure. Examples would be power transformers or synchronous machines operating in parallel modelled as a single aggregate power transformer or aggregate synchronous machine.  
The attribute is not used for EquivalentBranch, EquivalentShunt and EquivalentInjection.

#### <a name="RotatingMachineGeneratingUnit_oneOf_i0_EquipmentnetworkAnalysisEnabled"></a>5.1.35. Property `RotatingMachine > RotatingMachine.GeneratingUnit > oneOf > HydroGeneratingUnit > Equipment.networkAnalysisEnabled`

**Title:** networkAnalysisEnabled

|              |           |
| ------------ | --------- |
| **Type**     | `boolean` |
| **Required** | No        |

**Description:** The equipment is enabled to participate in network analysis.  If unspecified, the value is assumed to be true.

#### <a name="RotatingMachineGeneratingUnit_oneOf_i0_GeneratingUnittotalEfficiency"></a>5.1.36. Property `RotatingMachine > RotatingMachine.GeneratingUnit > oneOf > HydroGeneratingUnit > GeneratingUnit.totalEfficiency`

#### <a name="RotatingMachineGeneratingUnit_oneOf_i0_EquipmentnormallyInService"></a>5.1.37. Property `RotatingMachine > RotatingMachine.GeneratingUnit > oneOf > HydroGeneratingUnit > Equipment.normallyInService`

**Title:** normallyInService

|              |           |
| ------------ | --------- |
| **Type**     | `boolean` |
| **Required** | No        |

**Description:** Specifies the availability of the equipment under normal operating conditions. True means the equipment is available for topology processing, which determines if the equipment is energized or not. False means that the equipment is treated by network applications as if it is not in the model.

#### <a name="RotatingMachineGeneratingUnit_oneOf_i0_IdentifiedObjectmRID"></a>5.1.38. Property `RotatingMachine > RotatingMachine.GeneratingUnit > oneOf > HydroGeneratingUnit > IdentifiedObject.mRID`

**Title:** mRID

|              |          |
| ------------ | -------- |
| **Type**     | `string` |
| **Required** | No       |

**Description:** Master resource identifier issued by a model authority. The mRID is unique within an exchange context. Global uniqueness is easily achieved by using a UUID, as specified in RFC 4122, for the mRID. The use of UUID is strongly recommended.
For CIMXML data files in RDF syntax conforming to IEC 61970-552, the mRID is mapped to rdf:ID or rdf:about attributes that identify CIM object elements.

#### <a name="RotatingMachineGeneratingUnit_oneOf_i1_GeneratingUnitGenUnitOpSchedule"></a>5.2.1. Property `RotatingMachine > RotatingMachine.GeneratingUnit > oneOf > SolarGeneratingUnit > GeneratingUnit.GenUnitOpSchedule`

|                           |                                                                                                             |
| ------------------------- | ----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| **Type**                  | `object`                                                                                                    |
| **Required**              | No                                                                                                          |
| **Additional properties** | [[Any type: allowed]](# "Additional Properties of any type are allowed.")                                   |
| **Same definition as**    | [GeneratingUnit.GenUnitOpSchedule](#RotatingMachineGeneratingUnit_oneOf_i0_GeneratingUnitGenUnitOpSchedule) |

**Description:** The generating unit's Operator-approved current operating schedule (or plan), typically produced with the aid of unit commitment type analyses. The X-axis represents absolute time. The Y1-axis represents the status (0=off-line and unavailable: 1=available: 2=must run: 3=must run at fixed power value: etc.). The Y2-axis represents the must run fixed power value where required.

#### <a name="RotatingMachineGeneratingUnit_oneOf_i1_GeneratingUnitGenUnitOpCostCurves"></a>5.2.2. Property `RotatingMachine > RotatingMachine.GeneratingUnit > oneOf > SolarGeneratingUnit > GeneratingUnit.GenUnitOpCostCurves`

**Title:** GenUnitOpCostCurve

|              |         |
| ------------ | ------- |
| **Type**     | `array` |
| **Required** | No      |

**Description:** Relationship between unit operating cost (Y-axis) and unit output active power (X-axis). The operating cost curve for thermal units is derived from heat input and fuel costs. The operating cost curve for hydro units is derived from water flow rates and equivalent water costs.

#### <a name="RotatingMachineGeneratingUnit_oneOf_i1_GeneratingUnitgovernorSCD"></a>5.2.4. Property `RotatingMachine > RotatingMachine.GeneratingUnit > oneOf > SolarGeneratingUnit > GeneratingUnit.governorSCD`

**Title:** governorSCD

|                        |                                                                                                 |
| ---------------------- | ----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| **Type**               | `object or number`                                                                              |
| **Required**           | No                                                                                              |
| **Same definition as** | [GeneratingUnit.governorSCD](#RotatingMachineGeneratingUnit_oneOf_i0_GeneratingUnitgovernorSCD) |

**Description:** Governor Speed Changer Droop.   This is the change in generator power output divided by the change in frequency normalized by the nominal power of the generator and the nominal frequency and expressed in percent and negated. A positive value of speed change droop provides additional generator output upon a drop in frequency.

#### <a name="RotatingMachineGeneratingUnit_oneOf_i1_GeneratingUnitnormalPF"></a>5.2.18. Property `RotatingMachine > RotatingMachine.GeneratingUnit > oneOf > SolarGeneratingUnit > GeneratingUnit.normalPF`

**Title:** normalPF

|              |          |
| ------------ | -------- |
| **Type**     | `number` |
| **Required** | No       |

**Description:** Generating unit economic participation factor.  The sum of the participation factors across generating units does not have to sum to one.  It is used for representing distributed slack participation factor. The attribute shall be a positive value or zero.

#### <a name="RotatingMachineGeneratingUnit_oneOf_i1_GeneratingUnitpenaltyFactor"></a>5.2.19. Property `RotatingMachine > RotatingMachine.GeneratingUnit > oneOf > SolarGeneratingUnit > GeneratingUnit.penaltyFactor`

**Title:** penaltyFactor

|              |          |
| ------------ | -------- |
| **Type**     | `number` |
| **Required** | No       |

**Description:** Defined as: 1 / ( 1 - Incremental Transmission Loss); with the Incremental Transmission Loss expressed as a plus or minus value. The typical range of penalty factors is (0.9 to 1.1).

#### <a name="RotatingMachineGeneratingUnit_oneOf_i1_Equipmentaggregate"></a>5.2.30. Property `RotatingMachine > RotatingMachine.GeneratingUnit > oneOf > SolarGeneratingUnit > Equipment.aggregate`

**Title:** aggregate

|              |           |
| ------------ | --------- |
| **Type**     | `boolean` |
| **Required** | No        |

**Description:** The aggregate flag provides an alternative way of representing an aggregated (equivalent) element. It is applicable in cases when the dedicated classes for equivalent equipment do not have all of the attributes necessary to represent the required level of detail.  In case the flag is set to “true” the single instance of equipment represents multiple pieces of equipment that have been modelled together as an aggregate equivalent obtained by a network reduction procedure. Examples would be power transformers or synchronous machines operating in parallel modelled as a single aggregate power transformer or aggregate synchronous machine.  
The attribute is not used for EquivalentBranch, EquivalentShunt and EquivalentInjection.

#### <a name="RotatingMachineGeneratingUnit_oneOf_i1_EquipmentnetworkAnalysisEnabled"></a>5.2.31. Property `RotatingMachine > RotatingMachine.GeneratingUnit > oneOf > SolarGeneratingUnit > Equipment.networkAnalysisEnabled`

**Title:** networkAnalysisEnabled

|              |           |
| ------------ | --------- |
| **Type**     | `boolean` |
| **Required** | No        |

**Description:** The equipment is enabled to participate in network analysis.  If unspecified, the value is assumed to be true.

#### <a name="RotatingMachineGeneratingUnit_oneOf_i1_GeneratingUnittotalEfficiency"></a>5.2.32. Property `RotatingMachine > RotatingMachine.GeneratingUnit > oneOf > SolarGeneratingUnit > GeneratingUnit.totalEfficiency`

#### <a name="RotatingMachineGeneratingUnit_oneOf_i1_EquipmentnormallyInService"></a>5.2.33. Property `RotatingMachine > RotatingMachine.GeneratingUnit > oneOf > SolarGeneratingUnit > Equipment.normallyInService`

**Title:** normallyInService

|              |           |
| ------------ | --------- |
| **Type**     | `boolean` |
| **Required** | No        |

**Description:** Specifies the availability of the equipment under normal operating conditions. True means the equipment is available for topology processing, which determines if the equipment is energized or not. False means that the equipment is treated by network applications as if it is not in the model.

#### <a name="RotatingMachineGeneratingUnit_oneOf_i1_IdentifiedObjectmRID"></a>5.2.34. Property `RotatingMachine > RotatingMachine.GeneratingUnit > oneOf > SolarGeneratingUnit > IdentifiedObject.mRID`

**Title:** mRID

|              |          |
| ------------ | -------- |
| **Type**     | `string` |
| **Required** | No       |

**Description:** Master resource identifier issued by a model authority. The mRID is unique within an exchange context. Global uniqueness is easily achieved by using a UUID, as specified in RFC 4122, for the mRID. The use of UUID is strongly recommended.
For CIMXML data files in RDF syntax conforming to IEC 61970-552, the mRID is mapped to rdf:ID or rdf:about attributes that identify CIM object elements.

#### <a name="RotatingMachineGeneratingUnit_oneOf_i2_GeneratingUnitGenUnitOpSchedule"></a>5.3.1. Property `RotatingMachine > RotatingMachine.GeneratingUnit > oneOf > NuclearGeneratingUnit > GeneratingUnit.GenUnitOpSchedule`

**Description:** The generating unit's Operator-approved current operating schedule (or plan), typically produced with the aid of unit commitment type analyses. The X-axis represents absolute time. The Y1-axis represents the status (0=off-line and unavailable: 1=available: 2=must run: 3=must run at fixed power value: etc.). The Y2-axis represents the must run fixed power value where required.

#### <a name="RotatingMachineGeneratingUnit_oneOf_i2_GeneratingUnitgovernorSCD"></a>5.3.4. Property `RotatingMachine > RotatingMachine.GeneratingUnit > oneOf > NuclearGeneratingUnit > GeneratingUnit.governorSCD`

**Title:** governorSCD

|                        |                                                                                                 |
| ---------------------- | ----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| **Type**               | `object or number`                                                                              |
| **Required**           | No                                                                                              |
| **Same definition as** | [GeneratingUnit.governorSCD](#RotatingMachineGeneratingUnit_oneOf_i0_GeneratingUnitgovernorSCD) |

**Description:** Governor Speed Changer Droop.   This is the change in generator power output divided by the change in frequency normalized by the nominal power of the generator and the nominal frequency and expressed in percent and negated. A positive value of speed change droop provides additional generator output upon a drop in frequency.

#### <a name="RotatingMachineGeneratingUnit_oneOf_i2_Equipmentaggregate"></a>5.3.30. Property `RotatingMachine > RotatingMachine.GeneratingUnit > oneOf > NuclearGeneratingUnit > Equipment.aggregate`

**Title:** aggregate

|              |           |
| ------------ | --------- |
| **Type**     | `boolean` |
| **Required** | No        |

**Description:** The aggregate flag provides an alternative way of representing an aggregated (equivalent) element. It is applicable in cases when the dedicated classes for equivalent equipment do not have all of the attributes necessary to represent the required level of detail.  In case the flag is set to “true” the single instance of equipment represents multiple pieces of equipment that have been modelled together as an aggregate equivalent obtained by a network reduction procedure. Examples would be power transformers or synchronous machines operating in parallel modelled as a single aggregate power transformer or aggregate synchronous machine.  
The attribute is not used for EquivalentBranch, EquivalentShunt and EquivalentInjection.

|              |           |
| ------------ | --------- |

False means that the equipment is treated by network applications as if it is not in the model.

#### <a name="RotatingMachineGeneratingUnit_oneOf_i2_IdentifiedObjectmRID"></a>5.3.34. Property `RotatingMachine > RotatingMachine.GeneratingUnit > oneOf > NuclearGeneratingUnit > IdentifiedObject.mRID`

**Title:** mRID

|              |          |
| ------------ | -------- |
| **Type**     | `string` |
| **Required** | No       |

**Description:** Master resource identifier issued by a model authority. The mRID is unique within an exchange context. Global uniqueness is easily achieved by using a UUID, as specified in RFC 4122, for the mRID. The use of UUID is strongly recommended.
For CIMXML data files in RDF syntax conforming to IEC 61970-552, the mRID is mapped to rdf:ID or rdf:about attributes that identify CIM object elements.

#### <a name="RotatingMachineGeneratingUnit_oneOf_i2_EquipmentinService"></a>5.3.36. Property `RotatingMachine > RotatingMachine.GeneratingUnit > oneOf > NuclearGeneratingUnit > Equipment.inService`

**Title:** inService

|              |           |
| ------------ | --------- |
| **Type**     | `boolean` |
| **Required** | No        |

**Description:** Specifies the availability of the equipment. True means the equipment is available for topology processing, which determines if the equipment is energized or not. False means that the equipment is treated by network applications as if it is not in the model.

#### <a name="RotatingMachineGeneratingUnit_oneOf_i3_GeneratingUnitGenUnitOpSchedule"></a>5.4.1. Property `RotatingMachine > RotatingMachine.GeneratingUnit > oneOf > WindGeneratingUnit > GeneratingUnit.GenUnitOpSchedule`

| ------------------------- | ----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |

#### <a name="RotatingMachineGeneratingUnit_oneOf_i3_GeneratingUnitGenUnitOpCostCurves"></a>5.4.2. Property `RotatingMachine > RotatingMachine.GeneratingUnit > oneOf > WindGeneratingUnit > GeneratingUnit.GenUnitOpCostCurves`

**Title:** GenUnitOpCostCurve

|              |         |
| ------------ | ------- |
| **Type**     | `array` |
| **Required** | No      |

**Description:** Relationship between unit operating cost (Y-axis) and unit output active power (X-axis). The operating cost curve for thermal units is derived from heat input and fuel costs. The operating cost curve for hydro units is derived from water flow rates and equivalent water costs.

The operating cost curve for thermal units is derived from heat input and fuel costs. The operating cost curve for hydro units is derived from water flow rates and equivalent water costs. |

| **Required**           | No                                                                                              |
| **Same definition as** | [GeneratingUnit.governorMPL](#RotatingMachineGeneratingUnit_oneOf_i0_GeneratingUnitgovernorMPL) |

**Description:** Governor motor position limit.

#### <a name="RotatingMachineGeneratingUnit_oneOf_i3_GeneratingUnitgovernorSCD"></a>5.4.4. Property `RotatingMachine > RotatingMachine.GeneratingUnit > oneOf > WindGeneratingUnit > GeneratingUnit.governorSCD`

**Title:** governorSCD

|                        |                                                                                                 |
| ---------------------- | ----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| **Type**               | `object or number`                                                                              |
| **Required**           | No                                                                                              |
| **Same definition as** | [GeneratingUnit.governorSCD](#RotatingMachineGeneratingUnit_oneOf_i0_GeneratingUnitgovernorSCD) |

**Description:** Governor Speed Changer Droop.   This is the change in generator power output divided by the change in frequency normalized by the nominal power of the generator and the nominal frequency and expressed in percent and negated. A positive value of speed change droop provides additional generator output upon a drop in frequency.

| ------------ | -------- |
| **Type**     | `number` |
| **Required** | No       |

**Description:** Generating unit economic participation factor.  The sum of the participation factors across generating units does not have to sum to one.  It is used for representing distributed slack participation factor. The attribute shall be a positive value or zero.

#### <a name="RotatingMachineGeneratingUnit_oneOf_i3_GeneratingUnitpenaltyFactor"></a>5.4.19. Property `RotatingMachine > RotatingMachine.GeneratingUnit > oneOf > WindGeneratingUnit > GeneratingUnit.penaltyFactor`

**Title:** penaltyFactor

|              |          |
| ------------ | -------- |
| **Type**     | `number` |
| **Required** | No       |

**Description:** Defined as: 1 / ( 1 - Incremental Transmission Loss); with the Incremental Transmission Loss expressed as a plus or minus value. The typical range of penalty factors is (0.9 to 1.1).

#### <a name="RotatingMachineGeneratingUnit_oneOf_i3_Equipmentaggregate"></a>5.4.30. Property `RotatingMachine > RotatingMachine.GeneratingUnit > oneOf > WindGeneratingUnit > Equipment.aggregate`

**Title:** aggregate

|              |           |
| ------------ | --------- |
| **Type**     | `boolean` |
| **Required** | No        |

**Description:** The aggregate flag provides an alternative way of representing an aggregated (equivalent) element. It is applicable in cases when the dedicated classes for equivalent equipment do not have all of the attributes necessary to represent the required level of detail.  In case the flag is set to “true” the single instance of equipment represents multiple pieces of equipment that have been modelled together as an aggregate equivalent obtained by a network reduction procedure. Examples would be power transformers or synchronous machines operating in parallel modelled as a single aggregate power transformer or aggregate synchronous machine.  
The attribute is not used for EquivalentBranch, EquivalentShunt and EquivalentInjection.

#### <a name="RotatingMachineGeneratingUnit_oneOf_i3_EquipmentnetworkAnalysisEnabled"></a>5.4.31. Property `RotatingMachine > RotatingMachine.GeneratingUnit > oneOf > WindGeneratingUnit > Equipment.networkAnalysisEnabled`

|              |           |
| ------------ | --------- |
| **Type**     | `boolean` |
| **Required** | No        |

**Description:** The equipment is enabled to participate in network analysis.  If unspecified, the value is assumed to be true.

|              |           |

| **Required** | No        |

**Description:** Specifies the availability of the equipment under normal operating conditions. True means the equipment is available for topology processing, which determines if the equipment is energized or not. False means that the equipment is treated by network applications as if it is not in the model.

#### <a name="RotatingMachineGeneratingUnit_oneOf_i3_WindGeneratingUnitwindGenUnitType"></a>5.4.34. Property `RotatingMachine > RotatingMachine.GeneratingUnit > oneOf > WindGeneratingUnit > WindGeneratingUnit.windGenUnitType`

#### <a name="RotatingMachineGeneratingUnit_oneOf_i3_IdentifiedObjectmRID"></a>5.4.35. Property `RotatingMachine > RotatingMachine.GeneratingUnit > oneOf > WindGeneratingUnit > IdentifiedObject.mRID`

**Title:** mRID

|              |          |
| ------------ | -------- |
| **Type**     | `string` |
| **Required** | No       |

**Description:** Master resource identifier issued by a model authority. The mRID is unique within an exchange context. Global uniqueness is easily achieved by using a UUID, as specified in RFC 4122, for the mRID. The use of UUID is strongly recommended.
For CIMXML data files in RDF syntax conforming to IEC 61970-552, the mRID is mapped to rdf:ID or rdf:about attributes that identify CIM object elements.

#### <a name="RotatingMachineGeneratingUnit_oneOf_i3_GeneratingUnitgenControlMode"></a>5.4.47. Property `RotatingMachine > RotatingMachine.GeneratingUnit > oneOf > WindGeneratingUnit > GeneratingUnit.genControlMode`

#### <a name="RotatingMachineGeneratingUnit_oneOf_i4_GeneratingUnitGenUnitOpSchedule"></a>5.5.1. Property `RotatingMachine > RotatingMachine.GeneratingUnit > oneOf > ThermalGeneratingUnit > GeneratingUnit.GenUnitOpSchedule`

**Description:** Governor Speed Changer Droop. A positive value of speed change droop provides additional generator output upon a drop in frequency.

| **Required** | No       |

#### <a name="RotatingMachineGeneratingUnit_oneOf_i4_GeneratingUnitpenaltyFactor"></a>5.5.19. Property `RotatingMachine > RotatingMachine.GeneratingUnit > oneOf > ThermalGeneratingUnit > GeneratingUnit.penaltyFactor`

**Title:** penaltyFactor

|              |          |
| ------------ | -------- |
| **Type**     | `number` |
| **Required** | No       |

**Description:** Defined as: 1 / ( 1 - Incremental Transmission Loss); with the Incremental Transmission Loss expressed as a plus or minus value. The typical range of penalty factors is (0.9 to 1.1).

#### <a name="RotatingMachineGeneratingUnit_oneOf_i4_Equipmentaggregate"></a>5.5.30. Property `RotatingMachine > RotatingMachine.GeneratingUnit > oneOf > ThermalGeneratingUnit > Equipment.aggregate`

**Title:** aggregate

|              |           |
| ------------ | --------- |
| **Type**     | `boolean` |
| **Required** | No        |

**Description:** The aggregate flag provides an alternative way of representing an aggregated (equivalent) element. It is applicable in cases when the dedicated classes for equivalent equipment do not have all of the attributes necessary to represent the required level of detail.  In case the flag is set to “true” the single instance of equipment represents multiple pieces of equipment that have been modelled together as an aggregate equivalent obtained by a network reduction procedure. Examples would be power transformers or synchronous machines operating in parallel modelled as a single aggregate power transformer or aggregate synchronous machine.  
The attribute is not used for EquivalentBranch, EquivalentShunt and EquivalentInjection.

|              |           |
| ------------ | --------- |

| **Required** | No        |

**Description:** The equipment is enabled to participate in network analysis.  If unspecified, the value is assumed to be true.

| **Required**   | No                 |
| **Defined in** | ./CurrentFlow.json |

**Description:** Steady-state short-circuit current (in A for the profile) of generator with compound excitation during 3-phase short circuit.
- Ikk=0: Generator with no compound excitation.
- Ikk<>0: Generator with compound excitation.
Ikk is used to calculate the minimum steady-state short-circuit current for generators with compound excitation.
(4.6.1.2 in IEC 60909-0:2001).
Used only for single fed short circuit on a generator. (4.3.4.2. in IEC 60909-0:2001).

| Property                                           | Pattern | Type             | Deprecated | Definition                                                                                                                                                       | Title/Description |
| -------------------------------------------------- | ------- | ---------------- | ---------- | ---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- | ----------------- |
| - [multiplier](#SynchronousMachineikk_multiplier ) | No      | enum (of string) | No         | Same as [BasicIntervalSchedule.value2Multiplier](#RotatingMachineGeneratingUnit_oneOf_i0_GeneratingUnitGenUnitOpSchedule_BasicIntervalSchedulevalue2Multiplier ) | nan               |
| - [unit](#SynchronousMachineikk_unit )             | No      | enum (of string) | No         | Same as [unit](#RotatingMachineGeneratingUnit_oneOf_i0_GeneratingUnitGenUnitOpSchedule_RegularIntervalScheduletimeStep_unit )                                    | nan               |
| - [value](#SynchronousMachineikk_value )           | No      | number           | No         | -                                                                                                                                                                | nan               |

## <a name="Equipmentaggregate"></a>54. Property `RotatingMachine > Equipment.aggregate`

**Title:** aggregate

|              |           |
| ------------ | --------- |
| **Type**     | `boolean` |
| **Required** | No        |

**Description:** The aggregate flag provides an alternative way of representing an aggregated (equivalent) element. It is applicable in cases when the dedicated classes for equivalent equipment do not have all of the attributes necessary to represent the required level of detail.  In case the flag is set to “true” the single instance of equipment represents multiple pieces of equipment that have been modelled together as an aggregate equivalent obtained by a network reduction procedure. Examples would be power transformers or synchronous machines operating in parallel modelled as a single aggregate power transformer or aggregate synchronous machine.  
The attribute is not used for EquivalentBranch, EquivalentShunt and EquivalentInjection.
